#--------------------------------------------------
echo "System Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        name "DNSN-ISP_GW-RT-03"
        power-management
            peq 1
                peq-type apeq-dc-2000
                no shutdown
            exit
            peq 2
                peq-type apeq-dc-2000
                no shutdown
            exit
            peq 3
                peq-type apeq-dc-2000
                no shutdown
            exit
            peq 4
                peq-type apeq-dc-2000
                no shutdown
            exit
            peq 5
                peq-type apeq-dc-2000
                no shutdown
            exit
        exit
        load-balancing
            system-ip-load-balancing
        exit
        rollback
            rollback-location "cf3:\rollback\rollback"
            local-max-checkpoints 50
        exit
        snmp
            packet-size 9216
        exit
        time
            ntp
                ntp-server
                no shutdown
            exit
            sntp
                shutdown
            exit
            zone KST 09
        exit
    exit

echo "System Security Cpm Hw Filters, PKI, TLS and LDAP Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        security
            cpm-filter
                ip-filter
                    entry 10 create
                        action accept
                        description "NTP-Server"
                        match protocol udp
                            src-ip 220.103.209.192/32
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 20 create
                        action accept
                        description "NTP-Server"
                        match protocol udp
                            src-ip 220.103.209.193/32
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 100 create
                        action drop
                        description "NTP-Drop"
                        log 101
                        match protocol udp
                            src-port 123 65535
                        exit
                    exit
                    entry 101 create
                        action drop
                        description "NTP-Drop"
                        log 101
                        match protocol udp
                            dst-port 123 65535
                        exit
                    exit
                    no shutdown
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit

echo "System Sync-If-Timing Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    system
        sync-if-timing
            begin
            commit
        exit
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "LAG Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    lag 1
        description "DNSN-ISP-DDOS-L3SW-01-LAG1"
        mode access
        port 1/1/10
        port 1/2/9
        port 1/2/10
        port 3/1/10
        port 3/2/9
        port 3/2/10
        port 5/1/10
        port 5/2/9
        port 5/2/10
        lacp passive administrative-key 32768
        port-threshold 2 action down
        no shutdown
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Redundancy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    redundancy
        synchronize config
        rollback-sync
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "QoS Policy Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    qos
        sap-ingress 10 name "FC_REMARK" create
            queue 1 create
            exit
            queue 11 multipoint create
            exit
            fc "be" create
                queue 1
                out-remark dscp be
            exit
        exit
        sap-egress 10 name "Rate-limit_Domestic" create
            queue 1 create
            exit
            policer 10 create
                rate 100000
                mbs 5 kilobytes
            exit
            ip-criteria
                entry 10 create
                    match protocol tcp
                        src-ip 203.236.1.247/32
                        src-port eq 80
                    exit
                    action policer 10 queue 1
                exit
            exit
        exit
    exit
#--------------------------------------------------
echo "Filter Configuration"
#--------------------------------------------------
    filter
        redirect-policy "NTP_PBR-ROUTE-TABLE" create
            destination 172.27.250.98 create
                ping-test
                    timeout 30
                    drop-count 5
                exit
                no shutdown
            exit
            no shutdown
        exit
        redirect-policy "SNS_PBR-ROUTE-TABLE" create
            destination 113.217.228.246 create
                ping-test
                    timeout 30
                    drop-count 5
                exit
                no shutdown
            exit
            no shutdown
        exit
        redirect-policy "SNS_IPv6_PBR-ROUTE-TABLE" create
            destination 2001:2d8::6:0:3 create
                ping-test
                    timeout 30
                    drop-count 5
                exit
                no shutdown
            exit
            no shutdown
        exit

            filter-name "INTERNET_FILTER"
            default-action forward
            description "INTERNET_FILTER"
